CREATE TABLE WB_BBS_FILE
(
  file_id      VARCHAR2(12) not null,
  create_date  DATE not null,
  file_name    VARCHAR2(255) not null,
  file_size    NUMBER(10) not null,
  file_content BLOB
);
alter table WB_BBS_FILE
  add primary key (FILE_ID);
CREATE TABLE WB_BBS_POST
(
  bbs_id    VARCHAR2(12) not null,
  post_date DATE not null,
  post_user VARCHAR2(12) not null,
  post_id   VARCHAR2(12) not null,
  content   CLOB
);
create index WB_BBS_POST_IDX1 on WB_BBS_POST (BBS_ID, POST_DATE);
create index WB_BBS_POST_IDX2 on WB_BBS_POST (POST_USER);
CREATE TABLE WB_BBS_TITLE
(
  bbs_id      VARCHAR2(12) not null,
  title       VARCHAR2(255) not null,
  set_top     NUMBER(1) not null,
  create_date DATE not null,
  create_user VARCHAR2(12) not null,
  reply_count NUMBER(8) not null,
  view_count  NUMBER(8) not null,
  post_date   DATE not null,
  post_user   VARCHAR2(12) not null,
  content     CLOB
);
create index WB_BBS_TITLE_IDX1 on WB_BBS_TITLE (SET_TOP, POST_DATE);
create index WB_BBS_TITLE_IDX2 on WB_BBS_TITLE (CREATE_USER);
create index WB_BBS_TITLE_IDX3 on WB_BBS_TITLE (POST_USER);
alter table WB_BBS_TITLE
  add primary key (BBS_ID);
CREATE TABLE WB_CUST
(
  cust_id      VARCHAR2(12) not null,

);

  dmy NUMBER(1)
);
CREATE TABLE WB_KEY

(
   APP_ID               VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,

   LOGIN_URL            VARCHAR2(250),
   DB_URL               VARCHAR2(250),
   DB_USER              VARCHAR2(100),
   DB_PASSWORD          VARCHAR2(100),
   ATTRIBUTE1           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE2           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE3           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE4           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE5           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE6           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE7           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE8           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE9           VARCHAR2(250),

   LAST_UPDATE_DATE     DATE,
   LAST_UPDATED_BY      VARCHAR2(36),
   LAST_UPDATE_LOGIN    VARCHAR2(36),
   DB_TYPE              VARCHAR2(100),
   IN_XIP               VARCHAR2(10)         DEFAULT 'Y',
   VERSION              VARCHAR2(20),
   CONSTRAINT PK_XIP_PUB_APPS PRIMARY KEY (APP_ID)
);

   ATTRIBUTE1           VARCHAR2(250),

   ATTRIBUTE7           VARCHAR2(250),

   ATTRIBUTE9           VARCHAR2(250),

   CONSTRAINT FK_XIP_WF_APP_PRIVILEGE FOREIGN KEY (APP_ID)

);

CREATE TABLE XIP_PUB_EMP_ASG 
(
   ASG_ID               VARCHAR2(50)         NOT NULL,
   EMP_ID               VARCHAR2(50)         NOT NULL,
   POST_ID              VARCHAR2(50)         NOT NULL,
   DEPT_ID              VARCHAR2(50)         NOT NULL,
   ORG_ID               VARCHAR2(50)         NOT NULL,
   ENABLED              VARCHAR2(5)          DEFAULT 'Y' NOT NULL,
   LAST_UPDATE_DATE     DATE,
   LAST_UPDATED_BY      VARCHAR2(100),
   CREATION_DATE        DATE,
   CREATED_BY           VARCHAR2(100),
   LAST_UPDATE_LOGIN    VARCHAR2(100),
   POST_SEQ             VARCHAR2(3),
   CONSTRAINT PK_XIP_PUB_EMP_ASG PRIMARY KEY (ASG_ID),
   CONSTRAINT FK_XIP_PUB_EMP_ASG_02 FOREIGN KEY (POST_ID)
         REFERENCES XIP_PUB_POSTS (POST_ID)
         NOT DEFERRABLE,
   CONSTRAINT FK_XIP_PUB_EMP_ASG_04 FOREIGN KEY (ORG_ID)
         REFERENCES XIP_PUB_ORGS (ORG_ID)
         NOT DEFERRABLE,
   CONSTRAINT FK_XIP_PUB_EMP_ASG_01 FOREIGN KEY (EMP_ID)
         REFERENCES XIP_PUB_EMPS (EMP_ID)
         NOT DEFERRABLE,
   CONSTRAINT FK_XIP_PUB_EMP_ASG_03 FOREIGN KEY (DEPT_ID)
         REFERENCES XIP_PUB_DEPTS (DEPT_ID)
         NOT DEFERRABLE
);

   ATTRIBUTE9           VARCHAR2(250),

   CREATED_BY           VARCHAR2(36),
   LAST_UPDATE_DATE     DATE,
   LAST_UPDATED_BY      VARCHAR2(36),
   LAST_UPDATE_LOGIN    VARCHAR2(36),
   STATUS               VARCHAR2(36),

         NOT DEFERRABLE

(
   APP_ID               VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   ENTITY_ID            VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   ENTITY_CODE          VARCHAR2(100)        NOT NULL,
   ENTITY_NAME          VARCHAR2(200)        NOT NULL,
   ENTITY_DESC          VARCHAR2(500),
   ATTRIBUTE1           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE2           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE3           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE4           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE5           VARCHAR2(250)        DEFAULT 'Y',
   ATTRIBUTE6           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE7           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE8           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE9           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE10          VARCHAR2(250),
   CREATION_DATE        DATE,
   CREATED_BY           VARCHAR2(36),
   LAST_UPDATE_DATE     DATE,
   LAST_UPDATED_BY      VARCHAR2(36),
   LAST_UPDATE_LOGIN    VARCHAR2(36),
   CONSTRAINT PK_XIP_WF_ENTITIES PRIMARY KEY (ENTITY_ID),
   CONSTRAINT UK_XIP_WF_ENTITIES UNIQUE (ENTITY_CODE),
   CONSTRAINT FK_XIP_WF_ENTITIES FOREIGN KEY (APP_ID)
         REFERENCES XIP_PUB_APPS (APP_ID)
         NOT DEFERRABLE DISABLE
);

CREATE TABLE XIP_WF_ARCH_TASK 
(
   TASK_ID              VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   PROCESS_ID           VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   PROCESS_CODE         VARCHAR2(200)        NOT NULL,
   PROCESS_VERSION      NUMBER(8,0)          NOT NULL,
   INSTANCE_ID          VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   INSTANCE_CODE        VARCHAR2(200)        NOT NULL,
   ACT_ID               VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   ACT_CODE             VARCHAR2(200)        NOT NULL,
   ACT_NAME             VARCHAR2(500)        NOT NULL,
   TASK_TITLE           VARCHAR2(500)        NOT NULL,
   FROM_USER            VARCHAR2(100)        NOT NULL,
   ASSIGN_USER          VARCHAR2(100)        NOT NULL,
   EXECUTE_USER         VARCHAR2(100)        NOT NULL,
   TASK_STATE           VARCHAR2(20)         NOT NULL,
   FROM_TASK_ID         VARCHAR2(36),
   BEGIN_DATE           DATE                 NOT NULL,
   END_DATE             DATE,
   APPROVE_COMMENT      VARCHAR2(4000),
   DESCRIPTION          VARCHAR2(4000),
   CLOSE_CAUSE          VARCHAR2(50),
   CREATE_TYPE          VARCHAR2(50)         DEFAULT 'normal' NOT NULL,
   ATTRIBUTE1           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE2           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE3           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE4           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE5           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE6           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE7           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE8           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE9           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE10          VARCHAR2(250),
   CREATION_DATE        DATE,
   CREATED_BY           VARCHAR2(36),
   LAST_UPDATE_DATE     DATE,
   LAST_UPDATED_BY      VARCHAR2(36),
   LAST_UPDATE_LOGIN    VARCHAR2(36),
   RESULT               VARCHAR2(200),
   TASK_EFFECTIVE       VARCHAR2(3)          DEFAULT 'Y',
   CLOSED_LINE_TYPE     VARCHAR2(3),
   CONSTRAINT PK_WF_ARCH_TASK PRIMARY KEY (TASK_ID)
);

CREATE TABLE XIP_WF_INS_TASK 
(
   TASK_ID              VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   PROCESS_ID           VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   PROCESS_CODE         VARCHAR2(200)        NOT NULL,
   PROCESS_VERSION      NUMBER(8,0)          NOT NULL,
   INSTANCE_ID          VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   INSTANCE_CODE        VARCHAR2(200)        NOT NULL,
   ACT_ID               VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   ACT_CODE             VARCHAR2(200)        NOT NULL,
   ACT_NAME             VARCHAR2(500)        NOT NULL,
   TASK_TITLE           VARCHAR2(500)        NOT NULL,
   FROM_USER            VARCHAR2(100)        NOT NULL,
   ASSIGN_USER          VARCHAR2(100)        NOT NULL,
   EXECUTE_USER         VARCHAR2(100)        NOT NULL,
   TASK_STATE           VARCHAR2(20)         NOT NULL,
   FROM_TASK_ID         VARCHAR2(36),
   BEGIN_DATE           DATE                 NOT NULL,
   END_DATE             DATE,
   APPROVE_COMMENT      VARCHAR2(4000),
   DESCRIPTION          VARCHAR2(4000),
   CLOSE_CAUSE          VARCHAR2(50),
   CREATE_TYPE          VARCHAR2(50)         DEFAULT 'normal' NOT NULL,
   ATTRIBUTE1           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE2           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE3           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE4           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE5           VARCHAR2(250),

   ATTRIBUTE10          VARCHAR2(250),
   CREATION_DATE        DATE,
   CREATED_BY           VARCHAR2(36),
   LAST_UPDATE_DATE     DATE,
   LAST_UPDATED_BY      VARCHAR2(36),
   LAST_UPDATE_LOGIN    VARCHAR2(36),
   CONSTRAINT PK_XIP_WF_PROCESS_PROPERTIES PRIMARY KEY (PROCESS_ID, PROPERTY_CODE),
   CONSTRAINT FK_XIP_WF_PROCESS_PROPERTIES FOREIGN KEY (PROCESS_ID)
         REFERENCES XIP_WF_PROCESSES (PROCESS_ID)
         NOT DEFERRABLE
);

CREATE TABLE XIP_WF_USER_HOLIDAY 
(
   PRIVILEGE_ID         VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   MASTER_USER_ID       VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   PROXY_USER_ID        VARCHAR2(36)         NOT NULL,
   BEGIN_DATE           DATE                 NOT NULL,
   END_DATE             DATE                 NOT NULL,
   ATTRIBUTE1           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE2           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE3           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE4           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE5           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE6           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE7           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE8           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE9           VARCHAR2(250),
   ATTRIBUTE10          VARCHAR2(250),
   CREATION_DATE        DATE,
   CREATED_BY           VARCHAR2(36),
   LAST_UPDATE_DATE     DATE,
   LAST_UPDATED_BY      VARCHAR2(36),
   LAST_UPDATE_LOGIN    VARCHAR2(36),
   CONSTRAINT PK_XIP_WF_USER_HOLIDAY PRIMARY KEY (PRIVILEGE_ID),
   CONSTRAINT FK_XIP_PUB_USER_HOLIDAY FOREIGN KEY (MASTER_USER_ID)
         REFERENCES XIP_PUB_USERS (USER_ID)
         NOT DEFERRABLE,
   CONSTRAINT FK_XIP_PUB_USER_HOLIDAY_1 FOREIGN KEY (PROXY_USER_ID)
         REFERENCES XIP_PUB_USERS (USER_ID)
         NOT DEFERRABLE
);
